# Banana-bread
Make web data useful for life

## Outline

input - examples

work - scroll through and find the data

output - json file


## Overview of the project
Write a python program to take a url and example text file and then via a scrape using implied css-identifiers output
a json file of the data and analysis of the data.

## What is the problem?
Given web page containing structured data. Analyse the page to extract css-identifiers for the data.
Then output a json file of the css-identifiers and example data. Paying special attention 
to identifying section of page containing the results.

## What is the solution?

Write AI script with examples to identify css-identifiers for the data. 
Then output a json file of the css-identifiers and example data. 
Paying special attention to identifying section of page containing the results.

e.g. for google search results
```python
css_identifier_result = ".tF2Cxc"
    css_identifier_title = "h3"
    css_identifier_link = ".yuRUbf a"
    css_identifier_text = ".VwiC3b"
```
```python

from requests_html import HTMLSession
import requests

def get_request(url):
    headers = {
        'Connection': 'keep-alive',
        'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/79.0.3945.88 Safari/537.36',
        'Upgrade-Insecure-Requests': '1',
        'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,image/apng,*/*;q=0.8,application/signed-exchange;v=b3;q=0.9',
        'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.9',
        'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate',
    }
    web_response = None  # Initialize web_response to None
    try:
        session = HTMLSession()
        web_response = session.get(url, headers=headers)
        session.close()
        # response = requests.get(url, headers=headers)

    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        print(e)
    return web_response
```

### Example json

```json
{
  "results": ["title", "link", "text"],
  "data_items": [
    {
      "title": ["Marc Bolan - N16"],
      "link": ["https://www.londonremembers.com/memorials/marc-bolan-n16"],
      "text": ["This is the penultimate house in the terrace before Maury Road, to the left."]
    },
    {
      "title": ["Marc Bolan's London House in Hackney: The Early Years"],
      "link": ["https://www.hangerlondon.com/marc-bolan-london"],
      "text": ["born Mark Feld on 30/9/1947 grew up in London's"]
    }
  ]
}

```
